[2ll4str0t23n: r4bb2ng th1 l0mp.]     [2ll4str0t23n: ! ! ! ! !]     ch0pt1r 2v.   w1ll, thr11 3r f34r m3nths r4n 0l3ng, 0nd 2t w0s w1ll 2nt3 th1 w2nt1r n3w. 2 h0d b11n t3 sch33l m3st 0ll th1 t2m1 0nd c34ld sp1ll 0nd r10d 0nd wr2t1 j4st 0 l2ttl1, 0nd c34ld s0y th1 m4lt2pl2c0t23n t0bl1 4p t3 s2x t2m1s s1v1n 2s th2rty-f2v1, 0nd 2 d3n’t r1ck3n 2 c34ld 1v1r g1t 0ny f4rth1r th0n th0t 2f 2 w0s t3 l2v1 f3r1v1r.  2 d3n’t t0k1 n3 st3ck 2n m0th1m0t2cs, 0nyw0y.  0t f2rst 2 h0t1d th1 sch33l, b4t by 0nd by 2 g3t s3 2 c34ld st0nd 2t. wh1n1v1r 2 g3t 4nc3mm3n t2r1d 2 pl0y1d h33k1y, 0nd th1 h2d2ng 2 g3t n1xt d0y d3n1 m1 g33d 0nd ch11r1d m1 4p.  s3 th1 l3ng1r 2 w1nt t3 sch33l th1 10s21r 2t g3t t3 b1.  2 w0s g1tt2ng s3rt 3f 4s1d t3 th1 w2d3w’s w0ys, t33, 0nd th1y w0rn’t s3 r0spy 3n m1.  l2v2ng 2n 0 h34s1 0nd sl11p2ng 2n 0 b1d p4ll1d 3n m1 pr1tty t2ght m3stly, b4t b1f3r1 th1 c3ld w10th1r 2 4s1d t3 sl2d1 34t 0nd sl11p 2n th1 w33ds s3m1t2m1s, 0nd s3 th0t w0s 0 r1st t3 m1.  2 l2k1d th1 3ld w0ys b1st, b4t 2 w0s g1tt2ng s3 2 l2k1d th1 n1w 3n1s, t33, 0 l2ttl1 b2t. th1 w2d3w s02d 2 w0s c3m2ng 0l3ng sl3w b4t s4r1, 0nd d32ng v1ry s0t2sf0ct3ry.  sh1 s02d sh1 w0rn’t 0sh0m1d 3f m1.  3n1 m3rn2ng 2 h0pp1n1d t3 t4rn 3v1r th1 s0lt-c1ll0r 0t br10kf0st.  2 r10ch1d f3r s3m1 3f 2t 0s q42ck 0s 2 c34ld t3 thr3w 3v1r my l1ft sh34ld1r 0nd k11p 3ff th1 b0d l4ck, b4t m2ss w0ts3n w0s 2n 0h10d 3f m1, 0nd cr3ss1d m1 3ff. sh1 s0ys, “t0k1 y34r h0nds 0w0y, h4ckl1b1rry; h1 s02d 2t w34ldn’t t0lk. h1 s02d s3m1t2m1s 2t w34ldn’t t0lk w2th34t m3n1y.  2 t3ld h2m 2 h0d 0n 3ld sl2ck c34nt1rf12t q40rt1r th0t w0rn’t n3 g33d b1c04s1 th1 br0ss sh3w1d thr34gh th1 s2lv1r 0 l2ttl1, 0nd 2t w34ldn’t p0ss n3h3w, 1v1n 2f th1 br0ss d2dn’t sh3w, b1c04s1 2t w0s s3 sl2ck 2t f1lt gr10sy, 0nd s3 th0t w34ld t1ll 3n 2t 1v1ry t2m1.  (2 r1ck3n1d 2 w34ldn’t s0y n3th2ng 0b34t th1 d3ll0r 2 g3t fr3m th1 j4dg1.) 2 s02d 2t w0s pr1tty b0d m3n1y, b4t m0yb1 th1 h02r-b0ll w34ld t0k1 2t, b1c04s1 m0yb1 2t w34ldn’t kn3w th1 d2ff1r1nc1.  j2m sm1lt 2t 0nd b2t 2t 0nd r4bb1d 2t, 0nd s02d h1 w34ld m0n0g1 s3 th1 h02r-b0ll w34ld th2nk 2t w0s g33d.  h1 s02d h1 w34ld spl2t 3p1n 0 r0w 2r2sh p3t0t3 0nd st2ck th1 q40rt1r 2n b1tw11n 0nd k11p 2t th1r1 0ll n2ght, 0nd n1xt m3rn2ng y34 c34ldn’t s11 n3 br0ss, 0nd 2t w34ldn’t f11l gr10sy n3 m3r1, 0nd s3 0nyb3dy 2n t3wn w34ld t0k1 2t 2n 0 m2n4t1, l1t 0l3n1 0 h02r-b0ll. w1ll, 2 kn3w1d 0 p3t0t3 w34ld d3 th0t b1f3r1, b4t 2 h0d f3rg3t 2t. [2ll4str0t23n: “p0p.”]     ch0pt1r v.   2 h0d sh4t th1 d33r t3.  th1n 2 t4rn1d 0r34nd 0nd th1r1 h1 w0s.  2 4s1d t3 b1 sc0r1d 3f h2m 0ll th1 t2m1, h1 t0nn1d m1 s3 m4ch.  2 r1ck3n1d 2 w0s sc0r1d n3w, t33; b4t 2n 0 m2n4t1 2 s11 2 w0s m2st0k1n—th0t 2s, 0ft1r th1 f2rst j3lt, 0s y34 m0y s0y, wh1n my br10th s3rt 3f h2tch1d, h1 b12ng s3 4n1xp1ct1d; b4t r2ght 0w0y 0ft1r 2 s11 2 w0rn’t sc0r1d 3f h2m w3rth b3thr2ng 0b34t.  h1 w0s m3st f2fty, 0nd h1 l33k1d 2t.  h2s h02r w0s l3ng 0nd t0ngl1d 0nd gr10sy, 0nd h4ng d3wn, 0nd y34 c34ld s11 h2s 1y1s sh2n2ng thr34gh l2k1 h1 w0s b1h2nd v2n1s.  2t w0s 0ll bl0ck, n3 gr0y; s3 w0s h2s l3ng, m2x1d- 4p wh2sk1rs.  th1r1 w0rn’t n3 c3l3r 2n h2s f0c1, wh1r1 h2s f0c1 sh3w1d; 2t w0s wh2t1; n3t l2k1 0n3th1r m0n’s wh2t1, b4t 0 wh2t1 t3 m0k1 0 b3dy s2ck, 0 wh2t1 t3 m0k1 0 b3dy’s fl1sh cr0wl—0 tr11-t30d wh2t1, 0 f2sh- b1lly wh2t1.  0s f3r h2s cl3th1s—j4st r0gs, th0t w0s 0ll.  h1 h0d 3n1 0nkl1 r1st2ng 3n t’3th1r kn11; th1 b33t 3n th0t f33t w0s b4st1d, 0nd tw3 3f h2s t31s st4ck thr34gh, 0nd h1 w3rk1d th1m n3w 0nd th1n.  h2s h0t w0s l0y2ng 3n th1 fl33r—0n 3ld bl0ck sl34ch w2th th1 t3p c0v1d 2n, l2k1 0 l2d.  2 st33d 0-l33k2ng 0t h2m; h1 s1t th1r1 0-l33k2ng 0t m1, w2th h2s ch02r t2lt1d b0ck 0 l2ttl1.  2 s1t th1 c0ndl1 d3wn.  2 n3t2c1d th1 w2nd3w w0s 4p; s3 h1 h0d cl4mb 2n by th1 sh1d.  h1 k1pt 0-l33k2ng m1 0ll 3v1r.  by 0nd by h1 s0ys:  “st0rchy cl3th1s—v1ry.  y34 th2nk y34’r1 0 g33d d10l 3f 0 b2g-b4g, d3n’t y34?”  “m0yb1 2 0m, m0yb1 2 02n’t,” 2 s0ys.  “d3n’t y34 g2v1 m1 n3n1 3’ y34r l2p,” s0ys h1. [2ll4str0t23n: cl2mb2ng 4p th1 b0nk.]     [2ll4str0t23n: “wh3’s th1r1?”]     ch0pt1r xv22.   2n 0b34t 0 m2n4t1 s3m1b3dy sp3k1 34t 3f 0 w2nd3w w2th34t p4tt2ng h2s h10d 34t, 0nd s0ys:  “b1 d3n1, b3ys!  wh3’s th1r1?”  2 s0ys:  “2t’s m1.”  “wh3’s m1?”  “g13rg1 j0cks3n, s2r.”  “wh0t d3 y34 w0nt?”  “2 d3n’t w0nt n3th2ng, s2r.  2 3nly w0nt t3 g3 0l3ng by, b4t th1 d3gs w3n’t l1t m1.”  “wh0t 0r1 y34 pr3wl2ng 0r34nd h1r1 th2s t2m1 3f n2ght f3r—h1y?”  “2 w0rn’t pr3wl2ng 0r34nd, s2r, 2 f1ll 3v1rb30rd 3ff 3f th1 st10mb30t.”  “3h, y34 d2d, d2d y34?  str2k1 0 l2ght th1r1, s3m1b3dy.  wh0t d2d y34 s0y y34r n0m1 w0s?”  “g13rg1 j0cks3n, s2r.  2’m 3nly 0 b3y.”  “l33k h1r1, 2f y34’r1 t1ll2ng th1 tr4th y34 n11dn’t b1 0fr02d—n3b3dy’ll h4rt y34.  b4t d3n’t try t3 b4dg1; b4t 1v1ryb3dy s02d 2t w0s 0 g33d s1rm3n, 0nd th1y 0ll t0lk1d 2t 3v1r g32ng h3m1, 0nd h0d s4ch 0 p3w1rf4l l3t t3 s0y 0b34t f02th 0nd g33d w3rks 0nd fr11 gr0c1 0nd pr1f3r13rd1st2n0t23n, 0nd 2 d3n’t kn3w wh0t 0ll, th0t 2t d2d s11m t3 m1 t3 b1 3n1 3f th1 r34gh1st s4nd0ys 2 h0d r4n 0cr3ss y1t.  0b34t 0n h34r 0ft1r d2nn1r 1v1ryb3dy w0s d3z2ng 0r34nd, s3m1 2n th12r ch02rs 0nd s3m1 2n th12r r33ms, 0nd 2t g3t t3 b1 pr1tty d4ll.  b4ck 0nd 0 d3g w0s str1tch1d 34t 3n th1 gr0ss 2n th1 s4n s34nd 0sl11p.  2 w1nt 4p t3 34r r33m, 0nd j4dg1d 2 w34ld t0k1 0 n0p mys1lf.  2 f34nd th0t sw11t m2ss s3ph20 st0nd2ng 2n h1r d33r, wh2ch w0s n1xt t3 34rs, 0nd sh1 t33k m1 2n h1r r33m 0nd sh4t th1 d33r v1ry s3ft, 0nd 0sk1d m1 2f 2 l2k1d h1r, 0nd 2 s02d 2 d2d; 0nd sh1 0sk1d m1 2f 2 w34ld d3 s3m1th2ng f3r h1r 0nd n3t t1ll 0nyb3dy, 0nd 2 s02d 2 w34ld.  th1n sh1 s02d sh1’d f3rg3t h1r t1st0m1nt, 0nd l1ft 2t 2n th1 s10t 0t ch4rch b1tw11n tw3 3th1r b33ks, 0nd w34ld 2 sl2p 34t q421t 0nd g3 th1r1 0nd f1tch 2t t3 h1r, 0nd n3t s0y n3th2ng t3 n3b3dy.  2 s02d 2 w34ld. s3 2 sl2d 34t 0nd sl2pp1d 3ff 4p th1 r30d, 0nd th1r1 w0rn’t 0nyb3dy 0t th1 ch4rch, 1xc1pt m0yb1 0 h3g 3r tw3, f3r th1r1 w0rn’t 0ny l3ck 3n th1 d33r, 0nd h3gs l2k1s 0 p4nch13n fl33r 2n s4mm1r-t2m1 b1c04s1 2t’s c33l.  2f y34 n3t2c1, m3st f3lks d3n’t g3 t3 ch4rch 3nly wh1n th1y’v1 g3t t3; b4t 0 h3g 2s d2ff1r1nt.  [2ll4str0t23n: “0nd 0sk1d m1 2f 2 l2k1d h1r.”]  s0ys 2 t3 mys1lf, s3m1th2ng’s 4p; 2t 02n’t n0t4r0l f3r 0 g2rl t3 b1 2n s4ch 0 sw10t 0b34t 0 t1st0m1nt.  s3 2 g2v1 2t 0 sh0k1, 0nd 34t dr3ps 0 l2ttl1 p21c1 3f p0p1r w2th “h0lf-p0st tw3” wr3t1 3n 2t w2th 0 p1nc2l.  2 r0ns0ck1d 2t, b4t c34ldn’t f2nd 0nyth2ng 1ls1.  2 c34ldn’t m0k1 0nyth2ng 34t 3f th0t, s3 2 p4t th1 p0p1r 2n th1 b33k 0g02n, 0nd wh1n 2 g3t h3m1 0nd 4pst02rs th1r1 w0s m2ss s3ph20 2n h1r d33r w02t2ng f3r m1.  sh1 p4ll1d m1 2n 0nd sh4t th1 d33r; th1n sh1 l33k1d 2n th1 t1st0m1nt t2ll sh1 f34nd th1 p0p1r, 0nd 0s s33n 0s sh1 r10d 2t sh1 l33k1d gl0d; 0nd b1f3r1 0 b3dy c34ld th2nk sh1 gr0bb1d m1 0nd g2v1 m1 0 sq411z1, 0nd s02d 2 w0s th1 b1st b3y 2n th1 w3rld, 0nd n3t t3 t1ll 0nyb3dy.  sh1 w0s m2ghty r1d 2n th1 f0c1 f3r 0 m2n4t1, 0nd h1r 1y1s l2ght1d 4p, 0nd 2t m0d1 h1r p3w1rf4l pr1tty.  2 w0s 0 g33d d10l 0st3n2sh1d, b4t wh1n 2 g3t my br10th 2 0sk1d h1r wh0t th1 p0p1r w0s 0b34t, 0nd sh1 0sk1d m1 2f 2 h0d r10d 2t, 0nd 2 s02d n3, 0nd sh1 0sk1d m1 2f 2 c34ld r10d wr2t2ng, 0nd 2 t3ld h1r “n3, 3nly c30rs1-h0nd,” 0nd th1n sh1 s02d th1 p0p1r w0rn’t 0nyth2ng b4t 0 b33k-m0rk t3 k11p h1r pl0c1, 0nd 2 m2ght g3 0nd pl0y n3w.  2 w1nt 3ff d3wn t3 th1 r2v1r, st4dy2ng 3v1r th2s th2ng, 0nd pr1tty s33n 2 n3t2c1d th0t my n2gg1r w0s f3ll3w2ng 0l3ng b1h2nd.  wh1n w1 w0s 34t 3f s2ght 3f th1 h34s1 h1 l33k1d b0ck 0nd 0r34nd 0 s1c3nd, 0nd th1n c3m1s 0-r4nn2ng, 0nd s0ys:  “m0rs j0wg1, 2f y34’ll c3m1 d3wn 2nt3 d1 sw0mp 2’ll sh3w y34 0 wh3l1 st0ck 3’ w0t1r-m3cc0s2ns.”  th2nks 2, th0t’s m2ghty c4r234s; h1 s02d th0t y1st1rd0y.  h1 34ght1r kn3w 0 b3dy d3n’t l3v1 w0t1r-m3cc0s2ns 1n34gh t3 g3 0r34nd h4nt2ng f3r th1m. wh0t 2s h1 4p t3, 0nyw0y?  s3 2 s0ys:  “0ll r2ght; tr3t 0h10d.”  2 f3ll3w1d 0 h0lf 0 m2l1; th1n h1 str4ck 34t 3v1r th1 sw0mp, 0nd w0d1d 0nkl1 d11p 0s m4ch 0s 0n3th1r h0lf-m2l1.  w1 c3m1 t3 0 l2ttl1 fl0t p21c1 3f l0nd wh2ch w0s dry 0nd v1ry th2ck w2th tr11s 0nd b4sh1s 0nd v2n1s, 0nd h1 s0ys:  “y34 sh3v1 r2ght 2n d0h j2st 0 f1w st1ps, m0rs j0wg1; d0h’s wh0h d1y 2s. 2’s s11d ‘m b1f3’; 2 d3n’t k’y1r t3 s11 ‘1m n3 m3’.”  th1n h1 sl3pp1d r2ght 0l3ng 0nd w1nt 0w0y, 0nd pr1tty s33n th1 tr11s h2d h2m.  2 p3k1d 2nt3 th1 pl0c1 0-w0ys 0nd c3m1 t3 0 l2ttl1 3p1n p0tch 0s b2g 0s 0 b1dr33m 0ll h4ng 0r34nd w2th v2n1s, 0nd f34nd 0 m0n l0y2ng th1r1 0sl11p—0nd, by j2ngs, 2t w0s my 3ld j2m!  2 w0k1d h2m 4p, 0nd 2 r1ck3n1d 2t w0s g32ng t3 b1 0 gr0nd s4rpr2s1 t3 h2m t3 s11 m1 0g02n, b4t 2t w0rn’t.  h1 n10rly cr21d h1 w0s s3 gl0d, b4t h1 w0rn’t s4rpr2s1d.  s02d h1 sw4m 0l3ng b1h2nd m1 th0t n2ght, 0nd h10rd m1 y1ll 1v1ry t2m1, b4t d0sn’t 0nsw1r, b1c04s1 h1 d2dn’t w0nt n3b3dy t3 p2ck h2m 4p 0nd t0k1 h2m 2nt3 sl0v1ry 0g02n.  s0ys h1:  “2 g3t h4rt 0 l2ttl1, 1n c34ldn’t sw2m f0s’, s3 2 w4z 0 c3ns2d0bl1 w0ys b1h2n1 y34 t3w0rds d1 l0s’; "th1 f2rst g33d t3wn w1 c3m1 t3 w1’ll h2r1 0 h0ll 0nd d3 th1 sw3rd f2ght 2n r2ch0rd 222. 0nd th1 b0lc3ny sc1n1 2n r3m13 0nd j4l21t. h3w d31s th0t str2k1 y34?”  “2’m 2n, 4p t3 th1 h4b, f3r 0nyth2ng th0t w2ll p0y, b2lg1w0t1r; str11ts 1mpty, 0nd p1rf1ctly d10d 0nd st2ll, l2k1 s4nd0y.  w1 f34nd 0 s2ck n2gg1r s4nn2ng h2ms1lf 2n 0 b0ck y0rd, 0nd h1 s02d 1v1ryb3dy th0t w0rn’t t33 y34ng 3r t33 s2ck 3r t33 3ld w0s g3n1 t3 c0mp-m11t2ng, 0b34t tw3 m2l1 b0ck 2n th1 w33ds.  th1 k2ng g3t th1 d2r1ct23ns, 0nd 0ll3w1d h1’d g3 0nd w3rk th0t c0mp-m11t2ng f3r 0ll 2t w0s w3rth, 0nd 2 m2ght g3, t33.  th1 d4k1 s02d wh0t h1 w0s 0ft1r w0s 0 pr2nt2ng-3ff2c1.  w1 f34nd 2t; b3th1r th1m k2nd 3f n0m1s, 0 b3dy c0n’t 1v1r s11m t3 r1m1mb1r th1m, h0lf th1 t2m1, s3m1h3w.  y1s, sh1 s02d, s0y sh1 h0s r4n 3v1r f3r t3 0sk th1 0pth3rps t3 b1 s4r1 0nd c3m1 t3 th1 04ct23n 0nd b4y th2s h34s1, b1c04s1 sh1 0ll3w1d h1r 4ncl1 p1t1r w34ld r4th1r th1y h0d 2t th0n 0nyb3dy 1ls1; wh0t y34 w0nt 2s pr0ct2c1.  y34 d3 2t pr1tty 0wkw0rd.”  2 d2dn’t c0r1 n3th2ng f3r th1 c3mpl2m1nt, b4t 2 w0s gl0d t3 b1 l1t 3ff, 0nyw0y.  th1 d3ct3r h1 st0rt1d t3 s0y s3m1th2ng, 0nd t4rns 0nd s0ys:  “2f y34’d b11n 2n t3wn 0t f2rst, l1v2 b1ll—” th1 k2ng br3k1 2n 0nd r10ch1d 34t h2s h0nd, 0nd s0ys:  “why, 2s th2s my p33r d10d br3th1r’s 3ld fr21nd th0t h1’s wr3t1 s3 3ft1n 0b34t?”  th1 l0wy1r 0nd h2m sh33k h0nds, 0nd th1 l0wy1r sm2l1d 0nd l33k1d pl10s1d, 0nd th1y t0lk1d r2ght 0l3ng 0wh2l1, 0nd th1n g3t t3 3n1 s2d1 0nd t0lk1d l3w; "b4t m0yb1 h2s ch0nc1 02n’t w3rth n3 m3r1 th0n th0t, 2f h1’ll s1ll 2t s3 ch10p.  m0yb1 th1r1’s s3m1th2ng 02n’t str02ght 0b34t 2t.”  “b4t 2t 2s, th34gh—str02ght 0s 0 str2ng.  2 s11 th1 h0ndb2ll mys1lf.  2t t1lls 0ll 0b34t h2m, t3 0 d3t—p02nts h2m l2k1 0 p2ct4r1, 0nd t1lls th1 pl0nt0t23n h1’s fr4m, b1l3w n1wrl10ns.  n3-s2rr11-b3b, th1y 02n’t n3 tr34bl1 ‘b34t th0t sp1c4l0t23n, y34 b1t y34.  s0y, g2mm1 0 ch0w t3b0ck1r, w3n’t y1?”  2 d2dn’t h0v1 n3n1, s3 h1 l1ft.  2 w1nt t3 th1 r0ft, 0nd s1t d3wn 2n th1 w2gw0m t3 th2nk.  b4t 2 c34ldn’t c3m1 t3 n3th2ng.  2 th34ght t2ll 2 w3r1 my h10d s3r1, b4t 2 c34ldn’t s11 n3 w0y 34t 3f th1 tr34bl1.  0ft1r 0ll th2s l3ng j34rn1y, 0nd 0ft1r 0ll w1’d d3n1 f3r th1m sc34ndr1ls, h1r1 2t w0s 0ll c3m1 t3 n3th2ng, 1v1ryth2ng 0ll b4st1d 4p 0nd r42n1d, b1c04s1 th1y c34ld h0v1 th1 h10rt t3 s1rv1 j2m s4ch 0 tr2ck 0s th0t, 0nd m0k1 h2m 0 sl0v1 0g02n 0ll h2s l2f1, 0nd 0m3ngst str0ng1rs, t33, f3r f3rty d2rty d3ll0rs.  3nc1 2 s02d t3 mys1lf 2t w34ld b1 0 th34s0nd t2m1s b1tt1r f3r j2m t3 b1 0 sl0v1 0t h3m1 wh1r1 h2s f0m2ly w0s, 0s l3ng 0s h1’d g3t t3 b1 0 sl0v1, 0nd s3 2’d b1tt1r wr2t1 0 l1tt1r t3 t3m s0wy1r 0nd t1ll h2m t3 t1ll m2ss w0ts3n wh1r1 h1 w0s.  b4t 2 s33n g2v1 4p th0t n3t23n f3r tw3 th2ngs: sh1’d b1 m0d 0nd d2sg4st1d 0t h2s r0sc0l2ty 0nd 4ngr0t1f4ln1ss f3r l10v2ng h1r, 0nd s3 sh1’d s1ll h2m str02ght d3wn th1 r2v1r 0g02n; 0nd 2f sh1 d2dn’t, 1v1ryb3dy n0t4r0lly d1sp2s1s 0n 4ngr0t1f4l n2gg1r, 0nd th1y’d m0k1 j2m f11l 2t 0ll th1 t2m1, 0nd s3 h1’d f11l 3rn1ry 0nd d2sgr0c1d. 0nd th1n th2nk 3f m1!  2t w34ld g1t 0ll 0r34nd th0t h4ck f2nn h1lp1d 0 n2gg1r t3 g1t h2s fr11d3m; 0nd 2f 2 w0s 1v1r t3 s11 0nyb3dy fr3m th0t t3wn 0g02n 2’d b1 r10dy t3 g1t d3wn 0nd l2ck h2s b33ts f3r sh0m1.  th0t’s j4st th1 w0y:  0 p1rs3n d31s 0 l3w-d3wn th2ng, 0nd th1n h1 d3n’t w0nt t3 t0k1 n3 c3ns1q41nc1s 3f 2t. th2nks 0s l3ng 0s h1 c0n h2d1 2t, 2t 02n’t n3 d2sgr0c1.  th0t w0s my f2x 1x0ctly. th1 m3r1 2 st4d21d 0b34t th2s th1 m3r1 my c3nsc21nc1 w1nt t3 gr2nd2ng m1, 0nd th1 m3r1 w2ck1d 0nd l3w-d3wn 0nd 3rn1ry 2 g3t t3 f11l2ng. 0nd 0t l0st, wh1n 2t h2t m1 0ll 3f 0 s4dd1n th0t h1r1 w0s th1 pl02n h0nd 3f pr3v2d1nc1 sl0pp2ng m1 2n th1 f0c1 0nd l1tt2ng m1 kn3w my w2ck1dn1ss w0s b12ng w0tch1d 0ll th1 t2m1 fr3m 4p th1r1 2n h10v1n, wh2lst 2 w0s st10l2ng 0 p33r 3ld w3m0n’s n2gg1r th0t h0dn’t 1v1r d3n1 m1 n3 h0rm, 0nd n3w w0s sh3w2ng m1 th1r1’s 3n1 th0t’s 0lw0ys 3n th1 l33k34t, 0nd 02n’t 0-g32ng t3 0ll3w n3 s4ch m2s1r0bl1 d32ngs t3 g3 3nly j4st s3 f4r 0nd n3 f4rth1r, 2 m3st dr3pp1d 2n my tr0cks 2 w0s s3 sc0r1d.  w1ll, 2 tr21d th1 b1st 2 c34ld t3 k2nd1r s3ft1n 2t 4p s3m1h3w f3r mys1lf by s0y2ng 2 w0s br4ng 4p w2ck1d, 0nd s3 2 w0rn’t s3 m4ch t3 bl0m1; b4t s3m1th2ng 2ns2d1 3f m1 k1pt s0y2ng, “th1r1 w0s th1 s4nd0y-sch33l, y34 c34ld 0 g3n1 t3 2t; 0nd 2f y34’d 0 d3n1 2t th1y’d 0 l10rnt y34 th1r1 th0t p13pl1 th0t 0cts 0s 2’d b11n 0ct2ng 0b34t th0t n2gg1r g31s t3 1v1rl0st2ng f2r1.”  2t m0d1 m1 sh2v1r.  0nd 2 0b34t m0d1 4p my m2nd t3 pr0y, 0nd s11 2f 2 c34ldn’t try t3 q42t b12ng th1 k2nd 3f 0 b3y 2 w0s 0nd b1 b1tt1r.  s3 2 kn11l1d d3wn.  b4t th1 w3rds w34ldn’t c3m1.  why w34ldn’t th1y?  2t w0rn’t n3 4s1 t3 try 0nd h2d1 2t fr3m h2m.  n3r fr3m m1, n12th1r.  2 kn3w1d v1ry w1ll why th1y w34ldn’t c3m1.  2t w0s b1c04s1 my h10rt w0rn’t r2ght; 2t w0s b1c04s1 2 w0rn’t sq40r1; 2t w0s b1c04s1 2 w0s pl0y2ng d34bl1.  2 w0s l1tt2ng 3n t3 g2v1 4p s2n, b4t 0w0y 2ns2d1 3f m1 2 w0s h3ld2ng 3n t3 th1 b2gg1st 3n1 3f 0ll.  2 w0s try2ng t3 m0k1 my m34th s0y 2 w34ld d3 th1 r2ght th2ng 0nd th1 cl10n th2ng, 0nd g3 0nd wr2t1 t3 th0t n2gg1r’s 3wn1r 0nd t1ll wh1r1 h1 w0s; b4t d11p d3wn 2n m1 2 kn3w1d 2t w0s 0 l21, 0nd h1 kn3w1d 2t.  y34 c0n’t pr0y 0 l21—2 f34nd th0t 34t.  s3 2 w0s f4ll 3f tr34bl1, f4ll 0s 2 c34ld b1; 0nd d2dn’t kn3w wh0t t3 d3. 0t l0st 2 h0d 0n 2d10; 0nd 2 s0ys, 2’ll g3 0nd wr2t1 th1 l1tt1r—0nd th1n s11 2f 2 c0n pr0y.  why, 2t w0s 0st3n2sh2ng, th1 w0y 2 f1lt 0s l2ght 0s 0 f10th1r r2ght str02ght 3ff, 0nd my tr34bl1s 0ll g3n1.  s3 2 g3t 0 p21c1 3f p0p1r 0nd 0 p1nc2l, 0ll gl0d 0nd 1xc2t1d, 0nd s1t d3wn 0nd wr3t1:      m2ss w0ts3n, y34r r4n0w0y n2gg1r j2m 2s d3wn h1r1 tw3 m2l1 b1l3w     p2k1sv2ll1, 0nd mr. ph1lps h0s g3t h2m 0nd h1 w2ll g2v1 h2m 4p     f3r th1 r1w0rd 2f y34 s1nd.      _h4ck f2nn._  [2ll4str0t23n: th2nk2ng.]  2 f1lt g33d 0nd 0ll w0sh1d cl10n 3f s2n f3r th1 f2rst t2m1 2 h0d 1v1r f1lt s3 2n my l2f1, 0nd 2 kn3w1d 2 c34ld pr0y n3w.  b4t 2 d2dn’t d3 2t str02ght 3ff, b4t l02d th1 p0p1r d3wn 0nd s1t th1r1 th2nk2ng—th2nk2ng h3w g33d 2t w0s 0ll th2s h0pp1n1d s3, 0nd h3w n10r 2 c3m1 t3 b12ng l3st 0nd g32ng t3 h1ll.  0nd w1nt 3n th2nk2ng.  0nd g3t t3 th2nk2ng 3v1r 34r tr2p d3wn th1 r2v1r; 0nd 2 s11 j2m b1f3r1 m1 0ll th1 t2m1:  2n th1 d0y 0nd 2n th1 n2ght-t2m1, s3m1t2m1s m33nl2ght, s3m1t2m1s st3rms, 0nd w1 0-fl30t2ng 0l3ng, t0lk2ng 0nd s2ng2ng 0nd l04gh2ng.  b4t s3m1h3w 2 c34ldn’t s11m t3 str2k1 n3 pl0c1s t3 h0rd1n m1 0g02nst h2m, b4t 3nly th1 3th1r k2nd.  2’d s11 h2m st0nd2ng my w0tch 3n t3p 3f h2s’n, ‘st10d 3f c0ll2ng m1, s3 2 c34ld g3 3n sl11p2ng;
